[1:36:44] RevenG_lol: Feeding is a term that may sound new and foreign to you if you haven’t encountered this type of game before. Simply put, a feeder is a person who dies easily within a game. A player who dies more than he kills damages his team because he feeds the opposing team with skills, experience, money, and strength. By constantly dying, the feeder player harms his team because he weakens it and prevents him from strengthening enough to defeat the opposing team.
